    .status.error { background: #fed7d7; color: #742a2a; display: block; }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="info-box">
    <strong>Subaward Data</strong> shows actual subcontracts awarded by prime contractors. Use this to find primes who subcontract in your NAICS codes - potential teaming partners!
  </div>

  <div id="searchForm">
    <div class="section">
      <h3>Search Filters</h3>
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="agency">Awarding Agency:</label>
        <select id="agency">${agencyOptions}</select>
      </div>
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="naics">NAICS Code (optional):</label>
        <input type="text" id="naics" placeholder="e.g., 541512" value="541512">
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="section">
      <h3>Date Range</h3>
      <div class="date-row">
        <div class="form-group">
          <label for="fromDate">From Date:</label>
          <input type="text" id="fromDate" placeholder="yyyy-MM-dd">
        </div>
        <div class="form-group">
          <label for="toDate">To Date:</label>
          <input type="text" id="toDate" placeholder="yyyy-MM-dd">
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="section">
      <h3>Optional Filters</h3>
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="primeUei">Prime Contractor UEI (optional):</label>
        <input type="text" id="primeUei" placeholder="Search specific prime contractor">
      </div>
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="piid">Contract PIID (optional):</label>
        <input type="text" id="piid" placeholder="Specific contract number">
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="warning-box">
      <strong>Note:</strong> Uses your SAM.gov API key. Rate limit: 1,000 requests/day for most accounts.
    </div>

    <div class="button-row">
      <button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="google.script.host.close()">Cancel</button>
      <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="executeSearch()">Search Subawards</button>
    </div>
  </div>

  <div id="loading" class="loading">
    <div class="spinner"></div>
    <p>Searching Federal Subawards...</p>
  </div>

  <div id="status" class="status"></div>

  <script>
    window.onload = function() {
      const today = new Date();
      const sixMonthsAgo = new Date();
      sixMonthsAgo.setMonth(sixMonthsAgo.getMonth() - 6);
      document.getElementById('toDate').value = today.toISOString().split('T')[0];
      document.getElementById('fromDate').value = sixMonthsAgo.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    };

    function executeSearch() {
      const params = {
        agency: document.getElementById('agency').value,
        naics: document.getElementById('naics').value.trim(),
        fromDate: document.getElementById('fromDate').value,
        toDate: document.getElementById('toDate').value,
        primeUei: document.getElementById('primeUei').value.trim(),
        piid: document.getElementById('piid').value.trim()
      };

      document.getElementById('searchForm').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('loading').classList.add('show');

      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(onSuccess)
        .withFailureHandler(onError)
        .executeSubawardSearch(params);
    }

    function onSuccess(result) {
      document.getElementById('loading').classList.remove('show');
      const status = document.getElementById('status');
      status.className = 'status success';
      status.textContent = result;
      status.style.display = 'block';
      setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 2500);
    }

    function onError(error) {
      document.getElementById('loading').classList.remove('show');
      document.getElementById('searchForm').style.display = 'block';
      const status = document.getElementById('status');
      status.className = 'status error';
      status.textContent = 'Error: ' + error.message;
      status.style.display = 'block';
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>`;
}

/**
 * Execute Subaward Search using SAM.gov Acquisition Subaward Reporting API
 * API Docs: https://open.gsa.gov/api/acquisition-subaward-outbound-api/
 * Endpoint: https://api.sam.gov/prod/contract/v1/subcontracts/search
 */
function executeSubawardSearch(params) {
  try {
    // Get SAM.gov API key
    const apiKey = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('SAM_API_KEY');
    if (!apiKey) {
      throw new Error('SAM.gov API key required. Set it via Federal → Set SAM.gov API Key');
    }

    // Build URL with query parameters (GET request per API docs)
    let url = 'https://api.sam.gov/prod/contract/v1/subcontracts/search?';
    url += 'api_key=' + encodeURIComponent(apiKey);
    url += '&pageSize=500';
    url += '&pageNumber=0';
    url += '&status=Published';

    // Add agency filter (4-digit agency ID)
    if (params.agency) {
      url += '&agencyId=' + params.agency;
    }

    // Add date range (format: yyyy-MM-dd)
    if (params.fromDate) {
      url += '&fromDate=' + params.fromDate;
    }
    if (params.toDate) {
      url += '&toDate=' + params.toDate;
    }

    // Add contract PIID if provided
    if (params.piid) {
      url += '&PIID=' + encodeURIComponent(params.piid);
    }

    Logger.log('Subaward API URL: ' + url.replace(apiKey, 'API_KEY_HIDDEN'));

    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
      method: 'GET',
      muteHttpExceptions: true,
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    });

    const responseCode = response.getResponseCode();
    const responseText = response.getContentText();

    Logger.log('Subaward API response code: ' + responseCode);

    if (responseCode === 401) {
      throw new Error('Invalid API key. Please update your SAM.gov API key via Federal menu.');
    }
    if (responseCode === 400) {
      Logger.log('Bad request: ' + responseText);
      throw new Error('Bad request: ' + responseText.substring(0, 150));
    }
    if (responseCode !== 200) {
      throw new Error('API returned ' + responseCode + ': ' + responseText.substring(0, 200));
    }

    const data = JSON.parse(responseText);
    let results = data.data || [];

    Logger.log('Subaward API returned ' + results.length + ' results, total: ' + (data.totalRecords || 0));

    // Filter by NAICS if provided (API doesn't have direct NAICS filter parameter)
    if (params.naics && results.length > 0) {
      results = results.filter(r => {
        if (!r.primeNaics) return false;
        const naicsStr = String(r.primeNaics);
        return naicsStr.startsWith(params.naics) || naicsStr === params.naics;
      });
      Logger.log('After NAICS filter: ' + results.length + ' results');
    }

    // Write to sheet
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sheet = ss.getSheetByName('Subaward Data');
    if (!sheet) {
      sheet = ss.insertSheet('Subaward Data');
    }

    sheet.clear();
    const headers = [[
      'Date Found', 'Prime Contractor', 'Prime UEI', 'Subcontractor', 'Sub UEI',
      'Subaward Amount', 'Subaward Date', 'NAICS', 'Agency', 'Description', 'Contract PIID'
    ]];
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 11).setValues(headers).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#805ad5').setFontColor('#ffffff');

    if (results.length === 0) {
      logScrapeActivity('Subaward API', 'No results found');
      return 'No subawards found matching your criteria. Try:\n• Broader date range\n• Different agency\n• Remove NAICS filter';
    }

    const rows = results.slice(0, 200).map(r => [
      new Date(),
      r.primeEntityName || '',
      r.primeEntityUei || '',
      r.subEntityLegalBusinessName || '',
      r.subEntityUei || '',
      r.subAwardAmount || '',
      r.subAwardDate || '',
      r.primeNaics || '',
      r.primeOrganizationInfo || '',
      (r.subAwardDescription || r.descriptionOfRequirement || '').substring(0, 200),
      r.PIID || ''
    ]);

    sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, 11).setValues(rows);

    // Format currency column
    sheet.getRange(2, 6, rows.length, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0.00');

    for (let i = 1; i <= 11; i++) sheet.autoResizeColumn(i);
    sheet.activate();

    const totalRecords = data.totalRecords || results.length;
    logScrapeActivity('Subaward API', 'Found ' + totalRecords + ' subawards, showing ' + rows.length);
    return 'Found ' + totalRecords + ' subawards! Showing top ' + rows.length + ' in "Subaward Data" sheet.';

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Subaward API error: ' + e.message);
    throw new Error(e.message);
  }
}

// ============================================================================
// FREELANCE JOB BOARD INTEGRATIONS
// ============================================================================

/**
 * Search keywords for IT/consulting jobs
 */
const JOB_SEARCH_KEYWORDS = [
  'software', 'developer', 'engineer', 'data', 'cloud', 'devops',
  'automation', 'python', 'javascript', 'api', 'consulting', 'analyst'
];

/**
 * Search RemoteOK for jobs
 */
function searchRemoteOK() {
  try {
    const url = 'https://remoteok.com/api';
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
      muteHttpExceptions: true,
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    });

    if (response.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error('RemoteOK API returned ' + response.getResponseCode());
    }

    const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    // First item is metadata, rest are jobs
    const jobs = data.slice(1).filter(job => job.position && job.company);

    return jobs.map(job => ({
      source: 'RemoteOK',
      title: job.position || '',
      company: job.company || '',
      location: job.location || 'Remote',
      salary: job.salary_min && job.salary_max ? '$' + job.salary_min + '-$' + job.salary_max : '',
      tags: Array.isArray(job.tags) ? job.tags.join(', ') : '',
      date: job.date || '',
      url: job.url || ('https://remoteok.com/remote-jobs/' + job.slug),
      description: (job.description || '').replace(/<[^>]*>/g, '').substring(0, 200)
    }));

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('RemoteOK error: ' + e.message);
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Search Remotive for jobs
 */
function searchRemotive(category) {
  try {
    let url = 'https://remotive.com/api/remote-jobs';
    if (category) url += '?category=' + encodeURIComponent(category);

    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
      muteHttpExceptions: true,
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    });

    if (response.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error('Remotive API returned ' + response.getResponseCode());
    }

    const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    const jobs = data.jobs || [];

    return jobs.map(job => ({
      source: 'Remotive',
      title: job.title || '',
      company: job.company_name || '',
      location: job.candidate_required_location || 'Remote',
      salary: job.salary || '',
      tags: job.category || '',
      date: job.publication_date || '',
      url: job.url || '',
      description: (job.description || '').replace(/<[^>]*>/g, '').substring(0, 200)
    }));

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Remotive error: ' + e.message);
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Search Arbeitnow for jobs
 */
function searchArbeitnow() {
  try {
    const url = 'https://www.arbeitnow.com/api/job-board-api';
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
      muteHttpExceptions: true,
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    });

    if (response.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error('Arbeitnow API returned ' + response.getResponseCode());
    }

    const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    const jobs = data.data || [];

    return jobs.map(job => ({
      source: 'Arbeitnow',
      title: job.title || '',
      company: job.company_name || '',
      location: job.location || 'Remote',
      salary: '',
      tags: Array.isArray(job.tags) ? job.tags.join(', ') : '',
      date: job.created_at || '',
      url: job.url || '',
      description: (job.description || '').replace(/<[^>]*>/g, '').substring(0, 200)
    }));

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Arbeitnow error: ' + e.message);
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Search Jobicy for jobs
 */
function searchJobicy() {
  try {
    const url = 'https://jobicy.com/api/v2/remote-jobs?count=50&industry=engineering';
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
      muteHttpExceptions: true,
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    });

    if (response.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error('Jobicy API returned ' + response.getResponseCode());
    }

    const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    const jobs = data.jobs || [];

    return jobs.map(job => ({
      source: 'Jobicy',
      title: job.jobTitle || '',
      company: job.companyName || '',
      location: job.jobGeo || 'Remote',
      salary: job.annualSalaryMin && job.annualSalaryMax ?
        '$' + job.annualSalaryMin + '-$' + job.annualSalaryMax : '',
      tags: job.jobIndustry || '',
      date: job.pubDate || '',
      url: job.url || '',
      description: (job.jobDescription || '').replace(/<[^>]*>/g, '').substring(0, 200)
    }));

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Jobicy error: ' + e.message);
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Search ALL job boards and combine results
 */
function searchAllJobBoards() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  ui.alert('Searching Job Boards', 'Searching RemoteOK, Remotive, Arbeitnow, and Jobicy...\n\nThis may take 10-15 seconds.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);

  const allJobs = [];
  const locationFilter = getJobLocationFilter();

  // Search all sources
  Logger.log('Searching RemoteOK...');
  const remoteOKJobs = searchRemoteOK();
  allJobs.push(...filterJobsByLocation(remoteOKJobs, locationFilter));
  Logger.log('RemoteOK: ' + remoteOKJobs.length + ' jobs');

  Logger.log('Searching Remotive...');
  const remotiveJobs = searchRemotive('software-dev');
  allJobs.push(...filterJobsByLocation(remotiveJobs, locationFilter));
  Logger.log('Remotive: ' + remotiveJobs.length + ' jobs');

  Logger.log('Searching Arbeitnow...');
  const arbeitnowJobs = searchArbeitnow();
  allJobs.push(...filterJobsByLocation(arbeitnowJobs, locationFilter));
  Logger.log('Arbeitnow: ' + arbeitnowJobs.length + ' jobs');

  Logger.log('Searching Jobicy...');
  const jobicyJobs = searchJobicy();
  allJobs.push(...filterJobsByLocation(jobicyJobs, locationFilter));
  Logger.log('Jobicy: ' + jobicyJobs.length + ' jobs');

  // Write to sheet
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName('Job Board Results');
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet('Job Board Results');
  }

  sheet.clear();
  const headers = [['Date Scraped', 'Source', 'Title', 'Company', 'Location', 'Salary', 'Tags', 'Posted', 'URL']];
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 9).setValues(headers).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#e53e3e').setFontColor('#ffffff');

  if (allJobs.length === 0) {
    logScrapeActivity('Job Boards', 'No results found');
    showInfo('Job Boards', 'No jobs found. Try again later.');
    return;
  }

  const rows = allJobs.slice(0, 300).map(job => [
    new Date(),
    job.source,
    job.title,
    job.company,
    job.location,
    job.salary,
    job.tags,
    job.date,
    job.url
  ]);

  sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, 9).setValues(rows);
  for (let i = 1; i <= 9; i++) sheet.autoResizeColumn(i);
  sheet.activate();

  const summary = 'RemoteOK: ' + remoteOKJobs.length + ', Remotive: ' + remotiveJobs.length +
    ', Arbeitnow: ' + arbeitnowJobs.length + ', Jobicy: ' + jobicyJobs.length;
  logScrapeActivity('Job Boards (All)', summary);
  showSuccess('Found ' + allJobs.length + ' jobs from 4 sources! Results in "Job Board Results" sheet.');
}

/**
 * Get location filter keywords from settings
 * @returns {Array} Array of lowercase location keywords to match
 */
function getJobLocationFilter() {
  const settings = getSearchSettings();
  const locationString = settings['Job Boards']?.locations || 
    DEFAULT_SEARCH_SETTINGS['Job Boards'].locations;
  return locationString.split(',').map(loc => loc.trim().toLowerCase()).filter(loc => loc);
}

/**
 * Filter jobs by location - keeps remote jobs AND jobs matching location keywords
 * @param {Array} jobs - Array of job objects
 * @param {Array} locationKeywords - Array of lowercase location strings to match
 * @returns {Array} Filtered jobs
 */
function filterJobsByLocation(jobs, locationKeywords) {
  if (!locationKeywords || locationKeywords.length === 0) return jobs;
  
  return jobs.filter(job => {
    const jobLocation = String(job.location || '').toLowerCase();
    const jobTitle = String(job.title || '').toLowerCase();
    const jobTags = String(job.tags || '').toLowerCase();
    const combined = jobLocation + ' ' + jobTitle + ' ' + jobTags;
    
    // Always keep remote jobs
    if (jobLocation.includes('remote') || jobLocation.includes('anywhere') || 
        jobLocation.includes('worldwide') || jobLocation === '') {
      return true;
    }
    
    // Check if job matches any location keyword
    return locationKeywords.some(keyword => combined.includes(keyword));
  });
}

/**
 * Show Job Board Search Dialog
 */
function showJobBoardSearch() {
  const html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(getJobBoardSearchHTML())
    .setWidth(550)
    .setHeight(450);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, 'Remote Job Board Search');
}

/**
 * Search selected job boards only
 */
function searchSelectedJobBoards(sources) {
  const allJobs = [];
  const locationFilter = getJobLocationFilter();

  if (sources.includes('remoteok')) {
    allJobs.push(...filterJobsByLocation(searchRemoteOK(), locationFilter));
  }
  if (sources.includes('remotive')) {
    allJobs.push(...filterJobsByLocation(searchRemotive('software-dev'), locationFilter));
  }
  if (sources.includes('arbeitnow')) {
    allJobs.push(...filterJobsByLocation(searchArbeitnow(), locationFilter));
  }
  if (sources.includes('jobicy')) {
    allJobs.push(...filterJobsByLocation(searchJobicy(), locationFilter));
  }

  writeJobResults(allJobs, sources.join(', '));
}

/**
 * Write job results to sheet
 */
function writeJobResults(jobs, sourceName) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName('Job Board Results');
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet('Job Board Results');
  }

  sheet.clear();
  const headers = [['Date Scraped', 'Source', 'Title', 'Company', 'Location', 'Salary', 'Tags', 'Posted', 'URL']];
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 9).setValues(headers).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#e53e3e').setFontColor('#ffffff');

  if (jobs.length === 0) {
    logScrapeActivity('Job Boards', 'No results found');
    return;
  }

  const rows = jobs.slice(0, 300).map(job => [
    new Date(),
    job.source,
    job.title,
    job.company,
    job.location,
    job.salary,
    job.tags,
    job.date,
    job.url
  ]);

  sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, 9).setValues(rows);
  for (let i = 1; i <= 9; i++) sheet.autoResizeColumn(i);
  sheet.activate();

  logScrapeActivity('Job Boards (' + sourceName + ')', 'Found ' + jobs.length + ' jobs');
}

/**
 * Individual job board search wrappers for menu
 */
function searchRemoteOKOnly() {
  const jobs = searchRemoteOK();
  writeJobResults(jobs, 'RemoteOK');
  showSuccess('Found ' + jobs.length + ' jobs from RemoteOK!');
}

function searchRemotiveOnly() {
  const jobs = searchRemotive('software-dev');
  writeJobResults(jobs, 'Remotive');
  showSuccess('Found ' + jobs.length + ' jobs from Remotive!');
}

function searchArbeitnowOnly() {
  const jobs = searchArbeitnow();
  writeJobResults(jobs, 'Arbeitnow');
  showSuccess('Found ' + jobs.length + ' jobs from Arbeitnow!');
}

function searchJobicyOnly() {
  const jobs = searchJobicy();
  writeJobResults(jobs, 'Jobicy');
  showSuccess('Found ' + jobs.length + ' jobs from Jobicy!');
}

// ============================================================================
// UNIFIED FEDERAL SEARCH - RUN ALL
// ============================================================================

/**
 * Run all federal searches with hardcoded criteria
 * Designed for scheduled triggers or one-click comprehensive search
 */
/**
 * Run all federal searches using HARDCODED defaults (original behavior)
 * This uses the default NAICS codes and doesn't read from Settings sheet
 */
function runAllFederalSearches() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  // Use hardcoded NAICS codes directly
  const naicsCodes = ['541512', '541519', '541511', '518210', '541611'];

  const result = ui.alert(
    'Run All Federal Searches (Default)',
    'This will search:\n\n' +
    '• SAM.gov (SDVOSB opportunities)\n' +
    '• SAM.gov Subawards (Find Primes)\n' +
    '• USAspending.gov (Contract awards)\n' +
    '• Grants.gov (IT/Tech grants)\n' +
    '• SBIR.gov (Recent awards)\n\n' +
    'Using default NAICS codes: ' + naicsCodes.join(', ') + '\n\n' +
    'This may take 45-90 seconds. Continue?',
    ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO
  );

  if (result !== ui.Button.YES) return;

  const startTime = new Date();
  const results = {
    sam: 0,
    subaward: 0,
    usaspending: 0,
    grants: 0,
    sbir: 0
  };

  // Create summary sheet
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let summarySheet = ss.getSheetByName('Federal Search Summary');
  if (!summarySheet) {
    summarySheet = ss.insertSheet('Federal Search Summary');
  }

  try {
    // 1. SAM.gov SDVOSB Search - hardcoded defaults
    Logger.log('Running SAM.gov SDVOSB search...');
    const samParams = {
      title: '',
      naicsCodes: naicsCodes,
      setAside: 'SDVOSBC',
      ptypes: ['o', 'k', 'p'],
      postedFrom: getDateMonthsAgo(3),
      postedTo: getTodayFormatted(),
      status: 'active'
    };

    try {
      const samResult = executeSAMSearch(samParams);
      const samMatch = samResult.match(/Found (\d+)/);
      results.sam = samMatch ? parseInt(samMatch[1]) : 0;
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('SAM search error: ' + e.message);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(1000);

    // 2. SAM.gov Subaward Search - find prime contractors
    Logger.log('Running SAM.gov Subaward search...');
    const today = new Date();
    const sixMonthsAgo = new Date();
    sixMonthsAgo.setMonth(sixMonthsAgo.getMonth() - 6);

    const subawardParams = {
      agency: '9700', // DOD - most common for IT
      naics: '541512', // Computer Systems Design
      fromDate: sixMonthsAgo.toISOString().split('T')[0],
      toDate: today.toISOString().split('T')[0],
      primeUei: '',
      piid: ''
    };

    try {
      const subawardResult = executeSubawardSearch(subawardParams);
      const subawardMatch = subawardResult.match(/Found (\d+)/);
      results.subaward = subawardMatch ? parseInt(subawardMatch[1]) : 0;
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('Subaward search error: ' + e.message);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(1000);

    // 3. USAspending Search - hardcoded defaults
    Logger.log('Running USAspending search...');
    const oneYearAgo = new Date();
    oneYearAgo.setFullYear(today.getFullYear() - 1);

    const usaParams = {
      keyword: 'technology',
      agency: '',
      naicsCodes: naicsCodes,
      startDate: oneYearAgo.toISOString().split('T')[0],
      endDate: today.toISOString().split('T')[0],
      awardType: 'contracts'
    };

    try {
      const usaResult = executeUSAspendingSearch(usaParams);
      const usaMatch = usaResult.match(/Found (\d+)/);
      results.usaspending = usaMatch ? parseInt(usaMatch[1]) : 0;
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('USAspending error: ' + e.message);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(1000);

    // 3. Grants.gov Search - hardcoded defaults
    Logger.log('Running Grants.gov search...');
    const grantsParams = {
      keyword: 'technology',
      category: 'ST', // Science and Technology
      agency: '',
      statuses: ['posted']
    };

    try {
      const grantsResult = executeGrantsGovSearch(grantsParams);
      const grantsMatch = grantsResult.match(/Found (\d+)/);
      results.grants = grantsMatch ? parseInt(grantsMatch[1]) : 0;
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('Grants.gov error: ' + e.message);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(1000);

    // 4. SBIR.gov Search - hardcoded defaults
    Logger.log('Running SBIR.gov search...');
    const sbirParams = {
      agency: '',
      year: new Date().getFullYear().toString(),
      company: '',
      keyword: 'data'
    };

    try {
      const sbirResult = executeSBIRSearch(sbirParams);
      const sbirMatch = sbirResult.match(/Found (\d+)/);
      results.sbir = sbirMatch ? parseInt(sbirMatch[1]) : 0;
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('SBIR error: ' + e.message);
    }

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Unified search error: ' + e.message);
  }

  // Write summary
  const endTime = new Date();
  const duration = Math.round((endTime - startTime) / 1000);

  summarySheet.clear();
  summarySheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['Federal Search Summary', '', '', '']]).merge()
    .setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(14).setBackground('#1a365d').setFontColor('#ffffff');

  summarySheet.getRange(2, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['Last Run: ' + new Date().toLocaleString(), '', 'Duration: ' + duration + 's', '']]);

  summarySheet.getRange(4, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['Source', 'Results Found', 'Sheet Name', 'Status']])
    .setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#e2e8f0');

  summarySheet.getRange(5, 1, 5, 4).setValues([
    ['SAM.gov (SDVOSB)', results.sam, 'SAM.gov Data', results.sam > 0 ? 'Success' : 'No results'],
    ['SAM.gov Subawards', results.subaward, 'Subaward Data', results.subaward > 0 ? 'Success' : 'No results'],
    ['USAspending.gov', results.usaspending, 'USAspending Data', results.usaspending > 0 ? 'Success' : 'No results'],
    ['Grants.gov', results.grants, 'Grants.gov Data', results.grants > 0 ? 'Success' : 'No results'],
    ['SBIR.gov', results.sbir, 'SBIR.gov Data', results.sbir > 0 ? 'Success' : 'No results']
  ]);

  summarySheet.getRange(11, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['NAICS Codes Used: ' + naicsCodes.join(', '), '', '', '']]);

  for (let i = 1; i <= 4; i++) summarySheet.autoResizeColumn(i);
  summarySheet.activate();

  const totalResults = results.sam + results.subaward + results.usaspending + results.grants + results.sbir;
  logScrapeActivity('Federal (All)', 'Total: ' + totalResults + ' results in ' + duration + 's');

  showSuccess('Federal search complete!\n\n' +
    'SAM.gov: ' + results.sam + '\n' +
    'Subawards: ' + results.subaward + '\n' +
    'USAspending: ' + results.usaspending + '\n' +
    'Grants.gov: ' + results.grants + '\n' +
    'SBIR.gov: ' + results.sbir + '\n\n' +
    'Total: ' + totalResults + ' results in ' + duration + ' seconds');
}

/**
 * Run all federal searches using CUSTOM settings from Search Settings sheet
 * Use this when you want to test different keywords or NAICS codes
 */
function runFederalSearchesWithSettings() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  // Get settings from Search Settings sheet
  const settings = getSearchSettings();
  const samSettings = settings['SAM.gov'] || {};
  const usaSettings = settings['USAspending'] || {};
  const grantsSettings = settings['Grants.gov'] || {};
  const sbirSettings = settings['SBIR.gov'] || {};

  // Parse NAICS codes from settings (handle both camelCase and lowercase keys)
  const naicsString = samSettings.naicsCodes || samSettings.naicscodes || DEFAULT_SEARCH_SETTINGS['SAM.gov'].naicsCodes;
  const naicsCodes = naicsString.split(',').map(c => c.trim()).filter(c => c);

  const result = ui.alert(
    'Run Federal Searches (Custom Settings)',
    'This will search using your CUSTOM settings:\n\n' +
    '• SAM.gov (SDVOSB opportunities)\n' +
    '• USAspending.gov (Contract awards)\n' +
    '• Grants.gov (IT/Tech grants)\n' +
    '• SBIR.gov (Recent awards)\n\n' +
    'NAICS codes: ' + naicsCodes.join(', ') + '\n\n' +
    'Edit keywords in Settings menu to customize searches.\n\n' +
    'This may take 30-60 seconds. Continue?',
    ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO
  );

  if (result !== ui.Button.YES) return;

  const startTime = new Date();
  const results = {
    sam: 0,
    usaspending: 0,
    grants: 0,
    sbir: 0
  };

  // Create summary sheet
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let summarySheet = ss.getSheetByName('Federal Search Summary');
  if (!summarySheet) {
    summarySheet = ss.insertSheet('Federal Search Summary');
  }

  try {
    // 1. SAM.gov SDVOSB Search - using settings
    Logger.log('Running SAM.gov SDVOSB search with settings...');
    const samSetAside = samSettings.setAsidePreference || samSettings['set-asidePreference'] || DEFAULT_SEARCH_SETTINGS['SAM.gov'].setAside;
    const samKeywords = samSettings.keywords || DEFAULT_SEARCH_SETTINGS['SAM.gov'].keywords;

    const samParams = {
      title: samKeywords.split(',')[0].trim(),
      naicsCodes: naicsCodes,
      setAside: samSetAside,
      ptypes: ['o', 'k', 'p'],
      postedFrom: getDateMonthsAgo(3),
      postedTo: getTodayFormatted(),
      status: 'active'
    };

    try {
      const samResult = executeSAMSearch(samParams);
      const samMatch = samResult.match(/Found (\d+)/);
      results.sam = samMatch ? parseInt(samMatch[1]) : 0;
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('SAM search error: ' + e.message);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(1000);

    // 2. USAspending Search - using settings
    Logger.log('Running USAspending search with settings...');
    const today = new Date();
    const oneYearAgo = new Date();
    oneYearAgo.setFullYear(today.getFullYear() - 1);

    const usaNaicsString = usaSettings.naicsCodes || usaSettings.naicscodes || DEFAULT_SEARCH_SETTINGS['USAspending'].naicsCodes;
    const usaNaicsCodes = usaNaicsString.split(',').map(c => c.trim()).filter(c => c);
    const usaKeywords = usaSettings.keywords || DEFAULT_SEARCH_SETTINGS['USAspending'].keywords;

    const usaParams = {
      keyword: usaKeywords.split(',')[0].trim(),
      agency: '',
      naicsCodes: usaNaicsCodes,
      startDate: oneYearAgo.toISOString().split('T')[0],
      endDate: today.toISOString().split('T')[0],
      awardType: 'contracts'
    };

    try {
      const usaResult = executeUSAspendingSearch(usaParams);
      const usaMatch = usaResult.match(/Found (\d+)/);
      results.usaspending = usaMatch ? parseInt(usaMatch[1]) : 0;
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('USAspending error: ' + e.message);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(1000);

    // 3. Grants.gov Search - using settings
    Logger.log('Running Grants.gov search with settings...');
    const grantsKeyword = grantsSettings.keywords || DEFAULT_SEARCH_SETTINGS['Grants.gov'].keywords;
    const firstKeyword = grantsKeyword.split(',')[0].trim() || 'technology';

    const grantsParams = {
      keyword: firstKeyword,
      category: 'ST', // Science and Technology
      agency: grantsSettings.agencies || '',
      statuses: ['posted']
    };

    try {
      const grantsResult = executeGrantsGovSearch(grantsParams);
      const grantsMatch = grantsResult.match(/Found (\d+)/);
      results.grants = grantsMatch ? parseInt(grantsMatch[1]) : 0;
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('Grants.gov error: ' + e.message);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(1000);

    // 4. SBIR.gov Search - using settings
    Logger.log('Running SBIR.gov search with settings...');
    const sbirKeyword = sbirSettings.keywords || DEFAULT_SEARCH_SETTINGS['SBIR.gov'].keywords;
    const firstSbirKeyword = sbirKeyword.split(',')[0].trim();

    const sbirParams = {
      agency: sbirSettings.agencies || '',
      year: new Date().getFullYear().toString(),
      company: '',
      keyword: firstSbirKeyword
    };

    try {
      const sbirResult = executeSBIRSearch(sbirParams);
      const sbirMatch = sbirResult.match(/Found (\d+)/);
      results.sbir = sbirMatch ? parseInt(sbirMatch[1]) : 0;
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('SBIR error: ' + e.message);
    }

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Unified search error: ' + e.message);
  }

  // Write summary
  const endTime = new Date();
  const duration = Math.round((endTime - startTime) / 1000);

  summarySheet.clear();
  summarySheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['Federal Search Summary (Custom Settings)', '', '', '']]).merge()
    .setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(14).setBackground('#2c5282').setFontColor('#ffffff');

  summarySheet.getRange(2, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['Last Run: ' + new Date().toLocaleString(), '', 'Duration: ' + duration + 's', '']]);

  summarySheet.getRange(4, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['Source', 'Results Found', 'Sheet Name', 'Status']])
    .setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#e2e8f0');

  summarySheet.getRange(5, 1, 4, 4).setValues([
    ['SAM.gov (SDVOSB)', results.sam, 'SAM.gov Data', results.sam > 0 ? 'Success' : 'No results'],
    ['USAspending.gov', results.usaspending, 'USAspending Data', results.usaspending > 0 ? 'Success' : 'No results'],
    ['Grants.gov', results.grants, 'Grants.gov Data', results.grants > 0 ? 'Success' : 'No results'],
    ['SBIR.gov', results.sbir, 'SBIR.gov Data', results.sbir > 0 ? 'Success' : 'No results']
  ]);

  summarySheet.getRange(10, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['NAICS Codes Used: ' + naicsCodes.join(', '), '', '', '']]);
  summarySheet.getRange(11, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['(Using custom settings from Search Settings sheet)', '', '', '']]);

  for (let i = 1; i <= 4; i++) summarySheet.autoResizeColumn(i);
  summarySheet.activate();

  const totalResults = results.sam + results.usaspending + results.grants + results.sbir;
  logScrapeActivity('Federal (Custom)', 'Total: ' + totalResults + ' results in ' + duration + 's');

  showSuccess('Federal search complete (Custom Settings)!\n\n' +
    'SAM.gov: ' + results.sam + '\n' +
    'USAspending: ' + results.usaspending + '\n' +
    'Grants.gov: ' + results.grants + '\n' +
    'SBIR.gov: ' + results.sbir + '\n\n' +
    'Total: ' + totalResults + ' results in ' + duration + ' seconds');
}

/**
 * Run all job board searches (for triggers)
 */
function runAllJobBoardSearches() {
  searchAllJobBoards();
}

/**
 * Check your entity registration status on SAM.gov
 */
function checkSAMEntityStatus() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  const response = ui.prompt(
    'Check SAM Entity Status',
    'Enter UEI (Unique Entity ID) or DUNS number:',
    ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL
  );

  if (response.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return;

  const entityId = response.getResponseText().trim();

  try {
    const apiKey = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('SAM_API_KEY');
    const url = 'https://api.sam.gov/entity-information/v3/entities?' +
      'api_key=' + (apiKey || 'DEMO_KEY') +
      '&ueiSAM=' + entityId;

    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { muteHttpExceptions: true });

    if (response.getResponseCode() === 200) {
      const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

      if (data.entityData && data.entityData.length > 0) {
        const entity = data.entityData[0];
        const message = 'Entity Found!\n\n' +
          'Name: ' + (entity.entityRegistration?.legalBusinessName || 'N/A') + '\n' +
          'UEI: ' + (entity.entityRegistration?.ueiSAM || 'N/A') + '\n' +
          'Status: ' + (entity.entityRegistration?.registrationStatus || 'N/A') + '\n' +
          'Expiration: ' + (entity.entityRegistration?.registrationExpirationDate || 'N/A') + '\n' +
          'CAGE: ' + (entity.entityRegistration?.cageCode || 'N/A');

        ui.alert('SAM Entity Status', message, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        logScrapeActivity('SAM Entity', 'Checked: ' + entityId + ' - Found');
      } else {
        ui.alert('Not Found', 'No entity found with ID: ' + entityId, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        logScrapeActivity('SAM Entity', 'Checked: ' + entityId + ' - Not found');
      }
    } else {
      showError('SAM API error: ' + response.getResponseCode());
    }
  } catch (e) {
    showError('Could not check status: ' + e.message);
  }
}

function setSAMApiKey() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const response = ui.prompt(
    'Set SAM.gov API Key',
    'Enter your SAM.gov API key:\n(Register free at https://api.sam.gov)',
    ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL
  );

  if (response.getSelectedButton() === ui.Button.OK) {
    const key = response.getResponseText().trim();
    if (key) {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('SAM_API_KEY', key);
      showSuccess('SAM.gov API key saved securely');
    }
  }
}

function logScrapeActivity(source, activity) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.sheets.scrapeLog);

  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(CONFIG.sheets.scrapeLog);
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3).setValues([['Timestamp', 'Source', 'Activity']]).setFontWeight('bold');
  }

  sheet.appendRow([new Date(), source, activity]);
}

function viewScrapeLog() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.sheets.scrapeLog);

  if (sheet) {
    ss.setActiveSheet(sheet);
  } else {
    showInfo('Scrape Log', 'No scrape log found. Run a search first.');
  }
}

function getDateMonthsAgo(months) {
  const date = new Date();
  date.setMonth(date.getMonth() - months);
  return Utilities.formatDate(date, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'MM/dd/yyyy');
}

function getTodayFormatted() {
  return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'MM/dd/yyyy');
}

//============================================================================
// UTILITY FUNCTIONS
// ============================================================================

function backupAllData() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const timestamp = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd_HHmm');
  const backupName = ss.getName() + '_BACKUP_' + timestamp;

  Logger.log('Creating backup: ' + backupName);

  const backup = ss.copy(backupName);

  showSuccess('Backup created: ' + backupName + '\n\nLocation: Google Drive root folder');
}

function validateAllSheets() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();

  Logger.log('Validating all sheets...');

  let issues = [];
  let validated = 0;

  for (const sheet of sheets) {
    const name = sheet.getName();
    const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
    const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();

    if (lastRow === 0 || lastCol === 0) {
      issues.push(name + ': Sheet is empty');
    } else {
      validated++;
    }
  }

  let message = validated + ' sheets validated successfully';
  if (issues.length > 0) {
    message += '\n\nIssues found:\n' + issues.join('\n');
  }

  showInfo('Sheet Validation', message);
}

function formatAllHeaders() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();

  Logger.log('Formatting all headers...');

  let formatted = 0;

  for (const sheet of sheets) {
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();

    const headerWords = ['Category', 'Status', 'Priority', 'Service', 'Price', 'Name', '#', 'Action', 'Repository'];

    for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(10, data.length); i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      const isHeader = headerWords.some(word => row.some(cell => String(cell) === word));

      if (isHeader) {
        sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn())
          .setFontWeight('bold')
          .setBackground(CONFIG.colors.headerBg);
        formatted++;
        break;
      }
    }
  }

  showSuccess(formatted + ' headers formatted');
}

function clearAllHighlights() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getActiveSheet();

  Logger.log('Clearing highlights from: ' + sheet.getName());

  const range = sheet.getDataRange();
  range.setBackground(null);

  showSuccess('Highlights cleared from ' + sheet.getName());
}

// ============================================================================
// RUN ALL UPDATES
// ============================================================================

function runAllUpdates() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  const confirm = ui.alert(
    'Run All Updates',
    'This will run all update functions. Continue?',
    ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO
  );

  if (confirm !== ui.Button.YES) return;

  Logger.log('Running all updates...');

  const startTime = new Date();
  let completed = [];
  let errors = [];

  try {
    updateWeekDate();
    completed.push('Weekly Actions');
  } catch (e) {
    errors.push('Weekly: ' + e.message);
  }

  try {
    checkFederalDueDates();
    updateCertificationStatus();
    completed.push('Federal Contracting');
  } catch (e) {
    errors.push('Federal: ' + e.message);
  }

  const endTime = new Date();
  const duration = (endTime - startTime) / 1000;

  let message = 'Completed (' + duration.toFixed(1) + 's):\n• ' + completed.join('\n• ');
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    message += '\n\nErrors:\n• ' + errors.join('\n• ');
  }

  showInfo('All Updates Complete', message);
}

/**
 * Display a help dialog with HTML content
 */
function showHelpDialog(title, content, width, height) {
  width = width || 600;
  height = height || 500;

  const html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(getHelpStyles() + content)
    .setWidth(width)
    .setHeight(height);

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, title);
}

// ============================================================================
// HELPER FUNCTIONS

/**
 * Display error message to user
 * @param {string} message - Error message to display
 */
function showError(message) {
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('❌ Error', message, SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
  Logger.log('ERROR: ' + message);
}

/**
 * Display success message to user
 * @param {string} message - Success message to display
 */
function showSuccess(message) {
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('✅ Success', message, SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
  Logger.log('SUCCESS: ' + message);
}

/**
 * Display informational message to user
 * @param {string} title - Dialog title
 * @param {string} message - Message content
 */
function showInfo(title, message) {
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(title, message, SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
  Logger.log('INFO [' + title + ']: ' + message);
}

/**
 * Display warning message to user
 * @param {string} message - Warning message to display
 */
function showWarning(message) {
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('⚠️ Warning', message, SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
  Logger.log('WARNING: ' + message);
}

/**
 * Get the Monday of the week for a given date
 * @param {Date} date - Input date
 * @returns {Date} Monday of that week
 */
function getMonday(date) {
  const d = new Date(date);
  const day = d.getDay();
  const diff = d.getDate() - day + (day === 0 ? -6 : 1);
  return new Date(d.setDate(diff));
}

/**
 * Find the data range in a sheet based on a header keyword
 * @param {Sheet} sheet - Google Sheet object
 * @param {string} headerKeyword - Keyword to find in header row
 * @returns {Object|null} Object with headerRow, dataStart, dataEnd or null
 */
function findDataRange(sheet, headerKeyword) {
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  let headerRow = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (data[i].some(cell => String(cell) === headerKeyword)) {
      headerRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (headerRow === -1) {
    Logger.log('Header keyword "' + headerKeyword + '" not found in sheet');
    return null;
  }

  return {
    headerRow: headerRow,
    dataStart: headerRow + 1,
    dataEnd: sheet.getLastRow()
  };
}

/**
 * Count items by status in a given sheet
 * @param {string} sheetName - Name of the sheet
 * @param {string} statusColumnName - Name of the status column
 * @returns {Object} Object with status counts
 */
function countByStatus(sheetName, statusColumnName) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);

  if (!sheet) {
    Logger.log('Sheet not found: ' + sheetName);
    return {};
  }

  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const counts = {};
  let statusCol = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (statusCol === -1) {
      statusCol = data[i].indexOf(statusColumnName);
      continue;
    }
    if (statusCol >= 0) {
      const status = String(data[i][statusCol]).trim();
      if (status && status !== '') {
        counts[status] = (counts[status] || 0) + 1;
      }
    }
  }

  Logger.log('Counts for ' + sheetName + ': ' + JSON.stringify(counts));
  return counts;
}

/**
 * Gather counts from all tracked sheets
 * @returns {Object} Object with counts from all sheets
 */
function gatherAllCounts() {
  return {
    federal: countByStatus(CONFIG.sheets.federal, 'Status'),
    weekly: countByStatus(CONFIG.sheets.weekly, 'Status')
  };
}

/**
 * Apply priority-based colors to rows
 * @param {Sheet} sheet - Google Sheet object
 * @param {Object} dataRange - Data range object from findDataRange
 * @param {number} priorityCol - Column number (1-indexed) of priority column
 */
function applyPriorityColors(sheet, dataRange, priorityCol) {
  const numRows = dataRange.dataEnd - dataRange.dataStart + 1;
  if (numRows <= 0) return;

  const data = sheet.getRange(dataRange.dataStart, 1, numRows, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();

  for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    const priority = String(data[i][priorityCol - 1]).toUpperCase().trim();
    const row = dataRange.dataStart + i;
    const rowRange = sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn());

    if (priority === 'HIGH') {
      rowRange.setBackground(CONFIG.colors.high);
    } else if (priority === 'MEDIUM') {
      rowRange.setBackground(CONFIG.colors.medium);
    } else if (priority === 'LOW') {
      rowRange.setBackground(CONFIG.colors.low);
    }
  }

  Logger.log('Applied priority colors to ' + data.length + ' rows');
}

/**
 * Preview the dashboard color scheme
 * Creates a temporary sheet showing all colors
 */
function previewDashboardColors() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const colors = CONFIG.colors.dashboard;

  // Create or clear preview sheet
  let previewSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_Color Preview');
  if (previewSheet) {
    ss.deleteSheet(previewSheet);
  }
  previewSheet = ss.insertSheet('_Color Preview');

  // Set up the preview
  const data = [
    ['DASHBOARD COLOR SCHEME PREVIEW', '', '', ''],
    ['', '', '', ''],
    ['Color Name', 'Hex Code', 'Sample', 'Usage'],
    ['Title Bar', colors.titleBar, '', 'Main sheet titles (Row 1)'],
    ['Section Header', colors.sectionHeader, '', 'Section dividers'],
    ['Column Header', colors.columnHeader, '', 'Column headers'],
    ['Cell Background', colors.cellBackground, '', 'All data cells'],
    ['Alternating Row', colors.altRow, '', 'Every other row'],
    ['Border Color', colors.border, '', 'Subtle cell borders'],
    ['Accent Blue', colors.accentBlue, '', 'Highlights, links'],
    ['Accent Green', colors.accentGreen, '', 'Complete, success'],
    ['Accent Yellow', colors.accentYellow, '', 'Pending, warning'],
    ['Accent Red', colors.accentRed, '', 'Blocked, urgent'],
    ['', '', '', ''],
    ['STATUS COLORS', '', '', ''],
    ['High Priority', CONFIG.colors.high, '', 'HIGH priority items'],
    ['Medium Priority', CONFIG.colors.medium, '', 'MEDIUM priority items'],
    ['Low Priority', CONFIG.colors.low, '', 'LOW priority items'],
    ['Completed', CONFIG.colors.completed, '', 'Completed items'],
    ['Blocked', CONFIG.colors.blocked, '', 'Blocked items']
  ];

  previewSheet.getRange(1, 1, data.length, 4).setValues(data);

  // Format title
  previewSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4)
    .merge()
    .setBackground(colors.titleBar)
    .setFontColor(colors.headerText)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setFontSize(14)
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center');

  // Format column headers
  previewSheet.getRange(3, 1, 1, 4)
    .setBackground(colors.columnHeader)
    .setFontColor(colors.headerText)
    .setFontWeight('bold');

  // Apply color samples
  const colorRows = [
    [4, colors.titleBar],
    [5, colors.sectionHeader],
    [6, colors.columnHeader],
    [7, colors.cellBackground],
    [8, colors.altRow],
    [9, colors.border],
    [10, colors.accentBlue],
    [11, colors.accentGreen],
    [12, colors.accentYellow],
    [13, colors.accentRed],
    [16, CONFIG.colors.high],
    [17, CONFIG.colors.medium],
    [18, CONFIG.colors.low],
    [19, CONFIG.colors.completed],
    [20, CONFIG.colors.blocked]
  ];

  for (const [row, color] of colorRows) {
    previewSheet.getRange(row, 3).setBackground(color);
  }

  // Section header
  previewSheet.getRange(15, 1, 1, 4)
    .merge()
    .setBackground(colors.sectionHeader)
    .setFontColor(colors.headerText)
    .setFontWeight('bold');

  // Set column widths
  previewSheet.setColumnWidth(1, 150);
  previewSheet.setColumnWidth(2, 100);
  previewSheet.setColumnWidth(3, 80);
  previewSheet.setColumnWidth(4, 250);

  // Remove gridlines
  previewSheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  // Set light background for whole sheet
  previewSheet.getRange(1, 1, 25, 6).setBackground(colors.cellBackground);

  // Re-apply specific colors after background
  previewSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).setBackground(colors.titleBar);
  previewSheet.getRange(3, 1, 1, 4).setBackground(colors.columnHeader);
  previewSheet.getRange(15, 1, 1, 4).setBackground(colors.sectionHeader);
  for (const [row, color] of colorRows) {
    previewSheet.getRange(row, 3).setBackground(color);
  }

  ss.setActiveSheet(previewSheet);
  showSuccess('Color preview created! Check the "_Color Preview" sheet.');
}

/**
 * Apply LIGHT theme to current sheet
 */
function applyLightThemeToCurrentSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  applyThemeToSheet(sheet, 'light');
  showSuccess('Light theme applied to "' + sheet.getName() + '"');
}

/**
 * Apply DARK theme to current sheet
 */
function applyDarkThemeToCurrentSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  applyThemeToSheet(sheet, 'dark');
  showSuccess('Dark theme applied to "' + sheet.getName() + '"');
}

/**
 * Apply LIGHT theme to ALL sheets
 */
function applyLightThemeToAllSheets() {
  applyThemeToAllSheets('light');
}

/**
 * Apply DARK theme to ALL sheets
 */
function applyDarkThemeToAllSheets() {
  applyThemeToAllSheets('dark');
}

/**
 * Apply dashboard styling to the current sheet (backwards compatible)
 */
function applyDashboardStyleToCurrentSheet() {
  applyLightThemeToCurrentSheet();
}

/**
 * Apply dashboard styling to ALL sheets (backwards compatible)
 */
function applyDashboardStyleToAllSheets() {
  applyLightThemeToAllSheets();
}

/**
 * Apply a theme to ALL sheets
 * @param {string} themeName - 'light' or 'dark'
 */
function applyThemeToAllSheets(themeName) {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const themeLabel = themeName === 'dark' ? 'DARK' : 'LIGHT';
  const colors = themeName === 'dark' ? CONFIG.colors.dark : CONFIG.colors.light;

  const confirm = ui.alert(
    'Apply ' + themeLabel + ' Theme to All Sheets',
    'This will apply the ' + themeLabel + ' theme to ALL sheets:\n\n' +
    '• Remove gridlines\n' +
    '• Set ' + (themeName === 'dark' ? 'dark' : 'light') + ' background\n' +
    '• Style title rows\n' +
    '• Style section headers (TIER 1, TIER 2, etc.)\n' +
    '• Style column headers\n' +
    '• Add subtle borders\n\n' +
    'Continue?',
    ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO
  );

  if (confirm !== ui.Button.YES) return;

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();
  let styled = 0;
  let errors = [];

  for (const sheet of sheets) {
    if (sheet.getName().startsWith('_')) continue;

    try {
      applyThemeToSheet(sheet, themeName);
      styled++;
    } catch (e) {
      errors.push(sheet.getName() + ': ' + e.message);
    }
  }

  let message = 'Applied ' + themeLabel + ' theme to ' + styled + ' sheets.';
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    message += '\n\nErrors:\n• ' + errors.join('\n• ');
  }

  showInfo(themeLabel + ' Theme Applied', message);
}

/**
 * Apply a theme to a single sheet
 * @param {Sheet} sheet - Google Sheet object
 * @param {string} themeName - 'light' or 'dark'
 */
function applyThemeToSheet(sheet, themeName) {
  const sheetName = sheet.getName();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();

  if (lastRow === 0 || lastCol === 0) {
    Logger.log('Skipping empty sheet: ' + sheetName);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log('Applying ' + themeName + ' theme to: ' + sheetName);

  const colors = themeName === 'dark' ? CONFIG.colors.dark : CONFIG.colors.light;

  // 1. Remove gridlines
  sheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  // 2. Set background for entire data area (plus buffer)
  const maxRow = Math.max(lastRow + 20, 100);
  const maxCol = Math.max(lastCol + 5, 20);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, maxRow, maxCol).setBackground(colors.cellBackground);

  // 3. Set default text color for data area
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, maxRow, maxCol).setFontColor(colors.dataText);

  // 4. Find and style different header types - scan ALL rows
  const data = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).getValues();

  for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    const rowNum = i + 1;
    const rowData = data[i];
    const firstCell = String(rowData[0]).trim();
    const firstCellUpper = firstCell.toUpperCase();
    const rowText = rowData.join(' ').toUpperCase();
    const nonEmptyCells = rowData.filter(c => c !== '').length;

    // === TITLE ROW (Row 1 with main title) ===
    if (i === 0 && firstCell.length > 0) {
      if (rowText.includes('COMMAND CENTER') || rowText.includes('TNDS') ||
        rowText.includes('AUTOMATION') || rowText.includes('MODULES') ||
        rowText.includes('MASTER') ||
        (firstCellUpper === firstCell && firstCell.length > 10)) {
        sheet.getRange(rowNum, 1, 1, lastCol)
          .setBackground(colors.titleBar)
          .setFontColor(colors.headerText)
          .setFontWeight('bold')
          .setFontSize(12);
        continue;
      }
    }

    // === SECTION HEADERS (TIER 1:, TIER 2:, KEY METRICS, etc.) ===
    const isSectionHeader =
      // Starts with TIER followed by number
      /^TIER\s*\d/i.test(firstCell) ||
      // All caps section names
      (firstCellUpper === firstCell && firstCell.length > 5 &&
        nonEmptyCells <= 3 && !firstCell.includes('HTTP') &&
        !firstCell.includes('@') && !firstCell.includes('$')) ||
      // Known section patterns
      rowText.includes('STATUS OVERVIEW') ||
      rowText.includes('KEY METRICS') ||
      rowText.includes('UPGRADES') ||
      rowText.includes('SUMMARY') ||
      /^[A-Z\s\/]+:?\s*\(\$[\d,]+-?\$?[\d,]*\)/.test(firstCell); // "TIER 1: QUICK WINS ($500-$800)"

    if (isSectionHeader) {
      sheet.getRange(rowNum, 1, 1, lastCol)
        .setBackground(colors.sectionHeader)
        .setFontColor(colors.headerText)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setFontSize(11);
      continue;
    }

    // === COLUMN HEADERS (Price, Delivery, Description, etc.) ===
    const headerKeywords = [
      'Category', 'Status', 'Project', 'Metric', 'Item', '#',
      'Service', 'Repository', 'Action', 'Folder', 'Name',
      'Date', 'Title', 'Due', 'Owner', 'Current', 'Target',
      'Price', 'Delivery', 'Description', 'Notes', 'Upgrade',
      'Active', 'Pending', 'Blocked', 'Completed', 'Priority'
    ];
    const isHeaderRow = rowData.some(cell => {
      const cellStr = String(cell).trim();
      return headerKeywords.includes(cellStr) ||
        cellStr === 'Upgrade Path' ||
        cellStr === 'Priority Action';
    });

    if (isHeaderRow && nonEmptyCells >= 3) {
      sheet.getRange(rowNum, 1, 1, lastCol)
        .setBackground(colors.columnHeader)
        .setFontColor(colors.headerText)
        .setFontWeight('bold');
      continue;
    }
  }

  // 5. Add subtle borders to data area
  if (lastRow > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, colors.border, SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);
  }

  // 5. Freeze appropriate rows (first header row found)
  // Find first row with column headers
  for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(data.length, 10); i++) {
    const rowData = data[i];
    const headerKeywords = ['Category', 'Status', 'Project', 'Metric', 'Item', 'Service'];
    if (rowData.some(cell => headerKeywords.includes(String(cell).trim()))) {
      sheet.setFrozenRows(i + 1);
      break;
    }
  }

  Logger.log('Dashboard style applied to: ' + sheetName);
}

/**
 * Remove gridlines from current sheet only
 */
function removeGridlinesFromCurrentSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  sheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  showSuccess('Gridlines removed from "' + sheet.getName() + '"');
}

/**
 * Remove gridlines from all sheets
 */
function removeGridlinesFromAllSheets() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();

  for (const sheet of sheets) {
    sheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  }

  showSuccess('Gridlines removed from ' + sheets.length + ' sheets');
}

/**
 * Show gridlines on current sheet (undo)
 */
function showGridlinesOnCurrentSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  sheet.setHiddenGridlines(false);
  showSuccess('Gridlines restored on "' + sheet.getName() + '"');
}

/**
 * Apply light background to all cells in current sheet
 */
function applyLightBackgroundToCurrentSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  const colors = CONFIG.colors.dashboard;

  // Apply to a large range to cover all potential data
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 100, 26).setBackground(colors.cellBackground);

  showSuccess('Light background applied to "' + sheet.getName() + '"');
}

/**
 * Apply alternating row colors to current sheet
 */
function applyAlternatingRowsToCurrentSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();

  if (lastRow < 2 || lastCol === 0) {
    showError('Sheet has no data to format');
    return;
  }

  const colors = CONFIG.colors.dashboard;

  // Find the first data row (after headers)
  const data = sheet.getRange(1, 1, Math.min(10, lastRow), lastCol).getValues();
  let dataStartRow = 2;

  const headerKeywords = ['Category', 'Status', 'Project', 'Metric', '#'];
  for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (data[i].some(cell => headerKeywords.includes(String(cell).trim()))) {
      dataStartRow = i + 2;
      break;
    }
  }

  // Apply alternating colors
  for (let row = dataStartRow; row <= lastRow; row++) {
    const bgColor = (row - dataStartRow) % 2 === 0 ? colors.cellBackground : colors.altRow;
    sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, lastCol).setBackground(bgColor);
  }

  showSuccess('Alternating row colors applied');
}

// ============================================================================
// FORMATTING STANDARDIZATION
// ============================================================================

/**
 * Master function to standardize formatting across all sheets
 * Run this from menu: Utilities > Standardize All Formatting
 */
function standardizeAllFormatting() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  const confirm = ui.alert(
    'Standardize All Formatting',
    'This will apply consistent formatting to all sheets:\n\n' +
    '• Bold headers with blue background\n' +
    '• Freeze header rows\n' +
    '• Auto-resize columns\n' +
    '• Apply status colors\n' +
    '• Clean up borders\n\n' +
    'Continue?',
    ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO
  );

  if (confirm !== ui.Button.YES) return;

  Logger.log('Starting formatting standardization...');

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();
  let formatted = 0;
  let errors = [];

  for (const sheet of sheets) {
    try {
      formatSheet(sheet);
      formatted++;
    } catch (e) {
      errors.push(sheet.getName() + ': ' + e.message);
      Logger.log('Error formatting ' + sheet.getName() + ': ' + e.message);
    }
  }

  let message = 'Formatted ' + formatted + ' sheets successfully.';
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    message += '\n\nErrors:\n• ' + errors.join('\n• ');
  }

  showInfo('Formatting Complete', message);
}

/**
 * Format a single sheet with standard styling
 * @param {Sheet} sheet - Google Sheet object
 */
function formatSheet(sheet) {
  const sheetName = sheet.getName();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();

  if (lastRow === 0 || lastCol === 0) {
    Logger.log('Skipping empty sheet: ' + sheetName);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log('Formatting sheet: ' + sheetName);

  // Find header row (within first 5 rows)
  const topData = sheet.getRange(1, 1, Math.min(5, lastRow), lastCol).getValues();
  let headerRow = 1;

  const headerKeywords = ['#', 'Category', 'Status', 'Project', 'Service', 'Item',
    'Repository', 'Action', 'Folder', 'Date', 'Title', 'Notice'];

  for (let i = 0; i < topData.length; i++) {
    const hasHeader = topData[i].some(cell =>
      headerKeywords.includes(String(cell).trim())
    );
    if (hasHeader) {
      headerRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  // Format header row
  const headerRange = sheet.getRange(headerRow, 1, 1, lastCol);
  headerRange
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setBackground(CONFIG.colors.headerBg)
    .setFontColor('#1a1a1a')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle')
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center');

  // Freeze header row
  sheet.setFrozenRows(headerRow);

  // Apply borders to data range
  if (lastRow > headerRow) {
    const dataRange = sheet.getRange(headerRow, 1, lastRow - headerRow + 1, lastCol);
    dataRange.setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, '#d0d0d0', SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);
  }

  // Auto-resize columns (up to 12 columns max)
  for (let col = 1; col <= Math.min(lastCol, 12); col++) {
    sheet.autoResizeColumn(col);
    // Set minimum width
    if (sheet.getColumnWidth(col) < 80) {
      sheet.setColumnWidth(col, 80);
    }
    // Set maximum width
    if (sheet.getColumnWidth(col) > 300) {
      sheet.setColumnWidth(col, 300);
    }
  }

  // Apply status colors if Status column exists
  const headers = sheet.getRange(headerRow, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0];
  const statusCol = headers.indexOf('Status');

  if (statusCol >= 0 && lastRow > headerRow) {
    applyStatusColors(sheet, headerRow, statusCol + 1, lastRow);
  }

  // Apply priority colors if Priority column exists
  const priorityCol = headers.indexOf('Priority');
  if (priorityCol >= 0 && lastRow > headerRow) {
    applyPriorityColorsToColumn(sheet, headerRow, priorityCol + 1, lastRow);
  }

  Logger.log('Completed formatting: ' + sheetName);
}

/**
 * Apply colors based on status values
 * @param {Sheet} sheet - Google Sheet object
 * @param {number} headerRow - Header row number
 * @param {number} statusCol - Status column number (1-indexed)
 * @param {number} lastRow - Last row with data
 */
function applyStatusColors(sheet, headerRow, statusCol, lastRow) {
  const numRows = lastRow - headerRow;
  if (numRows <= 0) return;

  const statusData = sheet.getRange(headerRow + 1, statusCol, numRows, 1).getValues();

  for (let i = 0; i < statusData.length; i++) {
    const status = String(statusData[i][0]).toLowerCase().trim();
    const row = headerRow + 1 + i;
    const cell = sheet.getRange(row, statusCol);

    if (status.includes('complete') || status.includes('done') ||
      status.includes('active') || status.includes('approved')) {
      cell.setBackground('#d9ead3'); // Green
    } else if (status.includes('progress') || status.includes('pending') ||
      status.includes('todo') || status.includes('recent')) {
      cell.setBackground('#fff2cc'); // Yellow
    } else if (status.includes('blocked') || status.includes('overdue') ||
      status.includes('dormant') || status.includes('stale')) {
      cell.setBackground('#f4cccc'); // Red
    }
  }
}

/**
 * Apply colors based on priority values
 * @param {Sheet} sheet - Google Sheet object
 * @param {number} headerRow - Header row number
 * @param {number} priorityCol - Priority column number (1-indexed)
 * @param {number} lastRow - Last row with data
 */
function applyPriorityColorsToColumn(sheet, headerRow, priorityCol, lastRow) {
  const numRows = lastRow - headerRow;
  if (numRows <= 0) return;

  const priorityData = sheet.getRange(headerRow + 1, priorityCol, numRows, 1).getValues();

  for (let i = 0; i < priorityData.length; i++) {
    const priority = String(priorityData[i][0]).toUpperCase().trim();
    const row = headerRow + 1 + i;
    const cell = sheet.getRange(row, priorityCol);

    if (priority === 'HIGH') {
      cell.setBackground('#f4cccc').setFontWeight('bold');
    } else if (priority === 'MEDIUM') {
      cell.setBackground('#fff2cc');
    } else if (priority === 'LOW') {
      cell.setBackground('#d9ead3');
    }
  }
}

/**
 * Format a specific sheet by name
 */
function formatSpecificSheet() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const sheetNames = ss.getSheets().map(s => s.getName()).join('\n');

  const response = ui.prompt(
    'Format Specific Sheet',
    'Available sheets:\n' + sheetNames + '\n\nEnter sheet name:',
    ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL
  );

  if (response.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return;

  const sheetName = response.getResponseText().trim();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);

  if (!sheet) {
    showError('Sheet not found: ' + sheetName);
    return;
  }

  try {
    formatSheet(sheet);
    showSuccess('Sheet "' + sheetName + '" formatted successfully');
  } catch (e) {
    showError('Failed to format sheet: ' + e.message);
  }
}

/**
 * Create standard headers for a new sheet
 * @param {string} sheetType - Type of sheet (projects, weekly, pricing, github, federal, drive)
 */
function createStandardHeaders(sheetType) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getActiveSheet();

  const headerSets = {
    projects: ['Project', 'Status', 'Priority', 'Est Hours', 'Owner', 'Notes', 'Due Date'],
    weekly: ['#', 'Action Item', 'Status', 'Priority', 'Due', 'Owner', 'Notes'],
    pricing: ['Service', 'Description', 'Price', 'Unit', 'Category', 'Notes'],
    github: ['#', 'Repository', 'Language', 'Last Updated', 'Status', 'Visibility', 'Category', 'Purpose', 'Recommendation'],
    federal: ['Item', 'Type', 'Status', 'Due Date', 'Agency', 'Notes'],
    drive: ['Folder Name', 'URL', 'File Count', 'Last Updated', 'Notes']
  };

  const headers = headerSets[sheetType];
  if (!headers) {
    showError('Unknown sheet type: ' + sheetType);
    return;
  }

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
  formatSheet(sheet);
  showSuccess('Standard headers created for ' + sheetType + ' sheet');
}

/**
 * Add Formatting submenu to the main menu
 * Call this from onOpen to add formatting options
 */
function addFormattingMenu() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  ui.createMenu('🎨 Formatting')
    .addItem('Standardize All Sheets', 'standardizeAllFormatting')
    .addItem('Format Current Sheet', 'formatCurrentSheet')
    .addItem('Format Specific Sheet', 'formatSpecificSheet')
    .addSeparator()
    .addItem('Apply Status Colors', 'applyStatusColorsToCurrentSheet')
    .addItem('Apply Priority Colors', 'applyPriorityColorsToCurrentSheet')
    .addSeparator()
    .addSubMenu(ui.createMenu('Create Standard Headers')
      .addItem('Project Tracker', 'createProjectHeaders')
      .addItem('Weekly Actions', 'createWeeklyHeaders')
      .addItem('Pricing', 'createPricingHeaders')
      .addItem('GitHub Inventory', 'createGitHubHeaders')
      .addItem('Federal Contracting', 'createFederalHeaders')
      .addItem('Drive Index', 'createDriveHeaders'))
    .addToUi();
}

function formatCurrentSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  try {
    formatSheet(sheet);
    showSuccess('Sheet "' + sheet.getName() + '" formatted successfully');
  } catch (e) {
    showError('Failed to format sheet: ' + e.message);
  }
}

function applyStatusColorsToCurrentSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();

  if (lastRow < 2) {
    showError('Sheet has no data rows');
    return;
  }

  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0];
  const statusCol = headers.indexOf('Status');

  if (statusCol === -1) {
    showError('No "Status" column found');
    return;
  }

  applyStatusColors(sheet, 1, statusCol + 1, lastRow);
  showSuccess('Status colors applied');
}

function applyPriorityColorsToCurrentSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();

  if (lastRow < 2) {
    showError('Sheet has no data rows');
    return;
  }

  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0];
  const priorityCol = headers.indexOf('Priority');

  if (priorityCol === -1) {
    showError('No "Priority" column found');
    return;
  }

  applyPriorityColorsToColumn(sheet, 1, priorityCol + 1, lastRow);
  showSuccess('Priority colors applied');
}

/**

 * @param {string} theme - 'light' or 'dark'

  const isDark = theme === 'dark';

  return `
    <style>

        margin: 0;
      }

      .dashboard-container {
        padding: 16px;
        min-height: 100%;
      }

      .dashboard-header {
        background: ${isDark ? '#2d3748' : '#1a365d'};
        color: white;
        padding: 16px 20px;
        margin: -16px -16px 16px -16px;
        border-bottom: 3px solid ${isDark ? '#4a5568' : '#2c5282'};
      }

      .dashboard-header h1 {

        font-weight: 600;
        margin: 0 0 4px 0;
      }

      .dashboard-header .subtitle {
        font-size: 12px;
        opacity: 0.85;
      }

      .section {

        border-radius: 8px;

        box-shadow: 0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,${isDark ? '0.3' : '0.1'});

/**
 * Show Quick Stats Sidebar
 */
function showQuickStatsSidebar() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const theme = 'light';

  // Gather quick stats
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();
  const totalSheets = sheets.length;

  const weeklySheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.sheets.weekly);
  const weeklyCounts = weeklySheet ? countColumnValues(weeklySheet, 'Status') : {};
  const pendingTasks = (weeklyCounts['TODO'] || 0) + (weeklyCounts['Pending'] || 0) + (weeklyCounts['In Progress'] || 0);
  const completedTasks = (weeklyCounts['DONE'] || 0) + (weeklyCounts['Completed'] || 0) + (weeklyCounts['✓'] || 0);

  const federalSheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.sheets.federal);
  const federalCounts = federalSheet ? countColumnValues(federalSheet, 'Status') : {};
  const activeFederal = (federalCounts['Active'] || 0) + (federalCounts['In Progress'] || 0);

  const html = `
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head>
      <base target="_top">
      ${getDashboardCSS(theme)}
    </head>
    <body>
      <div class="sidebar-container">
        <div class="sidebar-header">
          <h2>⚡ Quick Stats</h2>
        </div>

        <div class="compact-stat">
          <span class="compact-stat-label">📊 Total Sheets</span>
          <span class="compact-stat-value">${totalSheets}</span>
        </div>

        <div class="compact-stat">
          <span class="compact-stat-label">📅 Pending Tasks</span>
          <span class="compact-stat-value" style="color: #d69e2e;">${pendingTasks}</span>
        </div>

        <div class="compact-stat">
          <span class="compact-stat-label">✓ Completed Tasks</span>
          <span class="compact-stat-value" style="color: #38a169;">${completedTasks}</span>
        </div>

        <div class="compact-stat">
          <span class="compact-stat-label">🏛️ Active Federal</span>
          <span class="compact-stat-value" style="color: #3182ce;">${activeFederal}</span>
        </div>

        <div style="margin-top: 16px;">
          ${pendingTasks > 10 ? '<div class="alert alert-warning">📅 ' + pendingTasks + ' tasks pending this week</div>' : ''}
          ${completedTasks > 0 ? '<div class="alert alert-success">✓ ' + completedTasks + ' tasks completed</div>' : ''}
        </div>

        <div class="last-updated" style="margin-top: 24px;">
          ${new Date().toLocaleString()}
        </div>
      </div>
    </body>
    </html>
  `;

  const htmlOutput = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(html)
    .setTitle('Quick Stats');

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showSidebar(htmlOutput);
}

/**
 * Show Weekly Actions Dashboard
 */
function showWeeklyActionsDashboard() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const theme = 'light';

  const weeklySheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.sheets.weekly);
  if (!weeklySheet) {
    showError('Weekly Actions sheet not found');
    return;
  }

  const data = weeklySheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];
  const actionCol = Math.max(headers.indexOf('Action Item'), headers.indexOf('Action'), 0);
  const statusCol = headers.indexOf('Status');
  const dueCol = headers.indexOf('Due');
  const ownerCol = headers.indexOf('Owner');

  const counts = countColumnValues(weeklySheet, 'Status');
  const total = Object.values(counts).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
  const done = (counts['DONE'] || 0) + (counts['Completed'] || 0) + (counts['✓'] || 0);
  const pending = total - done;

  let taskRows = '';
  let pendingCount = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length && pendingCount < 10; i++) {
    const status = String(data[i][statusCol] || '').toUpperCase();
    if (status !== 'DONE' && status !== 'COMPLETED' && status !== '✓' && data[i][actionCol]) {
      const statusClass = status.includes('PROGRESS') ? 'status-active' :
        status.includes('BLOCK') ? 'status-blocked' : 'status-pending';
      taskRows += `
        <tr>
          <td>${data[i][actionCol]}</td>
          <td><span class="status-badge ${statusClass}">${data[i][statusCol] || 'TODO'}</span></td>
          <td>${data[i][dueCol] || ''}</td>
        </tr>
      `;
      pendingCount++;
    }
  }

  const html = `
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head>
      <base target="_top">
      ${getDashboardCSS(theme)}
    </head>
    <body>
      <div class="dashboard-container">
        <div class="dashboard-header">
          <h1>📅 Weekly Actions</h1>
          <div class="subtitle">Week of ${getMonday(new Date()).toLocaleDateString()}</div>
        </div>

        <div class="section">
          <div class="stat-grid">
            <div class="stat-card stat-blue">
              <div class="stat-value">${total}</div>
              <div class="stat-label">Total Tasks</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-card stat-green">
              <div class="stat-value">${done}</div>
              <div class="stat-label">Completed</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-card stat-yellow">
              <div class="stat-value">${pending}</div>
              <div class="stat-label">Remaining</div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div style="margin-top: 12px;">
            <div class="progress-bar">
              <div class="progress-fill" style="width: ${total > 0 ? (done / total * 100) : 0}%"></div>
            </div>
            <div style="text-align: center; margin-top: 6px; font-size: 12px; color: #718096;">
              ${total > 0 ? Math.round(done / total * 100) : 0}% Complete
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div class="section">
          <div class="section-title">Pending Tasks</div>
          <table>
            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th>Task</th>
                <th>Status</th>
                <th>Due</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              ${taskRows || '<tr><td colspan="3" style="text-align:center;">All tasks completed! 🎉</td></tr>'}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>

        <button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="google.script.host.close()">Close</button>
        <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="google.script.run.showWeeklyActionsDashboard()">Refresh</button>
      </div>
    </body>
    </html>
  `;

  const htmlOutput = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(html)
    .setWidth(550)
    .setHeight(550);

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(htmlOutput, 'Weekly Actions');
}

/**
 * Show Federal Contracting Dashboard
 */
function showFederalDashboard() {

  const federalCounts = federalSheet ? countColumnValues(federalSheet, 'Status') : {};

  const html = `
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head>
      <base target="_top">
      ${getDashboardCSS(theme)}
    </head>
    <body>
      <div class="dashboard-container">

          <div class="subtitle">Certifications & Opportunities</div>
        </div>

        <div class="section">
          <div class="section-title">Certification Status</div>
          <div class="stat-grid">
            <div class="stat-card stat-green">
              <div class="stat-value">${federalCounts['Active'] || federalCounts['Approved'] || 0}</div>
              <div class="stat-label">Active</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-card stat-yellow">

/**
 * Helper function to count values in a column
 */
function countColumnValues(sheet, columnName) {
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];
  const colIndex = headers.indexOf(columnName);

  if (colIndex === -1) return {};

  const counts = {};
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    const value = String(data[i][colIndex]).trim();
    if (value) {
      counts[value] = (counts[value] || 0) + 1;
    }
  }
  return counts;
}

// ============================================================================
// SHEET AUDIT & REPORT
// ============================================================================

/**
 * Generate a comprehensive audit report of all sheets
 */
function generateSheetAuditReport() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();

  Logger.log('Generating sheet audit report...');

  let report = [];
  report.push(['Sheet Name', 'Rows', 'Columns', 'Has Headers', 'Status Col', 'Priority Col', 'Issues']);

  for (const sheet of sheets) {
    const name = sheet.getName();
    const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
    const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();

    let hasHeaders = 'No';
    let statusCol = 'N/A';
    let priorityCol = 'N/A';
    let issues = [];

    if (lastRow > 0 && lastCol > 0) {
      const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0];
      const headerKeywords = ['Status', 'Priority', 'Project', 'Item', '#', 'Action'];
      hasHeaders = headers.some(h => headerKeywords.includes(String(h))) ? 'Yes' : 'No';

      const statusIdx = headers.indexOf('Status');
      const priorityIdx = headers.indexOf('Priority');

      statusCol = statusIdx >= 0 ? 'Col ' + (statusIdx + 1) : 'N/A';
      priorityCol = priorityIdx >= 0 ? 'Col ' + (priorityIdx + 1) : 'N/A';

      // Check for issues
      if (hasHeaders === 'No') issues.push('No standard headers');
      if (lastRow === 1) issues.push('Only headers, no data');
      if (sheet.getFrozenRows() === 0) issues.push('Headers not frozen');
    } else {
      issues.push('Empty sheet');
    }

    report.push([name, lastRow, lastCol, hasHeaders, statusCol, priorityCol, issues.join('; ') || 'None']);
  }

  // Create or update audit sheet
  let auditSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_Sheet Audit');
  if (!auditSheet) {
    auditSheet = ss.insertSheet('_Sheet Audit');
  } else {
    auditSheet.clear();
  }

  auditSheet.getRange(1, 1, report.length, report[0].length).setValues(report);
  formatSheet(auditSheet);

  ss.setActiveSheet(auditSheet);
  showSuccess('Audit report generated with ' + (sheets.length) + ' sheets analyzed');
}
